# Roadmap

Work top-to-bottom; `/dev-cycle` picks the first unchecked item. Check items off as they land (with tests). Keep milestones honest — an item isn't done until it works in the running app **and** over the control protocol.

## M0 — Foundation ✅
- [x] Repo scaffold, docs, agent fleet, skills
- [x] SPM monorepo: DAWCore / DAWEngine / DAWControl / AIServices / DAWApp
- [x] Domain model v0 (project, tracks, clips, transport, mixer state)
- [x] Control WebSocket server skeleton + command router
- [x] MCP server skeleton with core tool surface
- [x] App shell: dark theme, transport bar, glowing meter component

## M1 — Core audio engine ✅
- [x] Audio file import (wav/aiff/mp3/m4a) onto tracks
- [x] Sample-accurate multitrack playback via engine graph
- [x] Transport: play/stop/seek/loop region, position broadcast to UI + control clients
- [x] Per-track and master metering (peak/RMS) driving the glow meters
- [x] Master volume, per-track volume/pan/mute/solo wired to engine
- [x] Offline render (mixdown to wav) — `render.mixdown` command
- [x] Engine test harness: offline-render assertions (null test, gain test) — determinism null (exact 0.0) + unity-vs-source + gain suite; golden-master null noted as future addition

## M2 — Recording & project persistence
- [x] Record from default input onto armed tracks (`track.setArm`, `transport.record`, host-time-aligned takes) — no round-trip latency compensation yet (M4 PDC)
- [x] Input device enumeration/selection (`input.listDevices`, `input.setDevice`) — pinned-device capture fixed 2026-07-05 (benign config-change triage + first-buffer watchdog; live E2E green for default-uid pin, ZoomAudioDevice pin, and unpinned)
- [x] Punch in/out windows (`transport.setPunch`, writer accept-window)
- [x] Metronome/click with count-in
- [x] `.dawproj` bundle format: versioned JSON + media dir; open/save/autosave
- [x] Undo/redo across all commands (coalescing snapshot journal in DAWCore; `edit.undo`/`edit.redo`, Edit-menu ⌘Z/⇧⌘Z)

## M3 — MIDI & instruments
- [x] (i) MIDI domain + commands — `Clip.notes` payload (`MIDINote`: pitch/velocity/startBeat/lengthBeats, clamped, canonically ordered, mutually exclusive with audio media); `clip.addMIDI` / `clip.setNotes` / `clip.remove` on the control protocol (whole-array note set, per-clip undo coalescing); additive v1 persistence; instrument-track-only rule
- [x] (ii) Piano-roll editor (Simple + Pro views) — note draw/move/resize/velocity, snap grid, driving `clip.setNotes`; timeline clip lanes + `debug.captureUI` self-render verification
- [x] (iii) Sample-accurate MIDI scheduler — settles the sequencer clock decision (one `AVAudioSourceNode` per instrument track; host-delta live epoch / latched offline epoch), lock-free event delivery via an immutable schedule behind a C11 atomic pointer (`CAtomics` shim, ≥1 s retire bin), all-notes-off flush flag on every stop/seek/tempo/loop-wrap/reschedule, `InstrumentRendering` seam (AU-shaped for M3 vi) with EventCaptureInstrument + TestToneInstrument; validated by frame-exact offline event-timestamp tests
- [x] (iv) Built-in poly synth — 16-voice subtractive synth (PolyBLEP saw/square, triangle, sine; linear ADSR; Simper SVF low-pass) behind `InstrumentRendering`; `Track.instrument: InstrumentDescriptor?` (additive, nil ⇒ polySynth default), `track.setInstrument` control command + `track_set_instrument` MCP tool with partial-update semantics; RT-safe in-place param changes (atomic POD publish, held notes survive), kind switch = node rebuild + reschedule
- [x] (v) Built-in sampler — key zones (`SamplerZone`: audio file, root pitch, span, gain) under the same `InstrumentDescriptor`; pitched playback via linear-interp resampling (2^(Δsemitones/12) × rate ratio), one-shot mode, anti-click attack/release; zones structural (rebuild) vs scalars in-place (atomic); zone media joins the `.dawproj` bundle copy (relative `media/` refs, dedupe, `mediaFilesCopied`); `sampler` object on `track.setInstrument` + MCP
- [x] (vi-a) AU instrument hosting (headless) — `HostedAUInstrument` adapter behind the `InstrumentRendering` seam (our scheduler stays the only clock; events via `scheduleMIDIEventBlock` at in-quantum offsets; flush → CC123+120), `AUHostRegistry` (timeout-raced async prepare, strict-select/graceful-load: missing AU → silent placeholder + `status`), descriptor kind `audioUnit` with component identity + fullState base64 in `.dawproj`, `instrument.listAudioUnits` + `track.setInstrument audioUnit:` + MCP; `renderMixdown` now async (offline renders instantiate fresh AU instances); out-of-process AUv3 reliability deferred to M9 app bundling
- [x] (vi-b) AU plugin UI windows — `requestViewController`/v2 view hosting in floating glass-chrome windows; open/close over the control protocol — split 2026-07-10 per `docs/research/design-vi-b-au-windows.md` (DESIGN SETTLED — the implementation contract; unblocked by pkg-a's real app bundle):
  - [x] (vi-b-1) Plumbing + generic body — engine accessors for the live `AUAudioUnit` (concrete-class-only boundary exception) + registry `onRelease` invalidation seam; `plugin.openUI/closeUI/listOpenUIs` through a typed async `PluginUIControlling` seam (headless-honest errors); `PluginWindowLedger` (DAWAppKit, headless) + `PluginWindowManager`/`NSPanel` glass chrome (cyan/neutral, never violet); `AUGenericViewController` body only; `debug.captureUI {target:"plugin"}`; mixer/instrument open-window buttons; 3 MCP tools; headless suites + orchestrator live gate on system AUs (DLSMusicDevice/AUDelay), fully provable on the bare binary
  - [x] (vi-b-2) Vendor views — full resolution ladder (`requestViewController` w/ 5 s once-gate timeout race → v2 `kAudioUnitProperty_CocoaUI` via `AUAudioUnitV2Bridge` + `AUViewProbe` in DAWEngine → `AUGenericViewController` fallback, never-failing), `BodyHostViewController` wrapping the vendor `AUCocoaUIBase` view, v3 `preferredContentSize` sizing + `frameDidChangeNotification` resize-follow (reentrancy-guarded, clamped in-bounds); §10 de-risk spike resolved by inventory (NO AUv3 installed — the out-of-process AUv3 custom-view leg is SKIPPED-recorded, never faked); live gate on system units proves both branches — DLSMusicDevice/AUDelay → `body:"custom"` (real vendor views inside our chrome), AUMatrixReverb → `body:"generic"` — bare binary AND `dist/DAWPro.app` bundle identity; `docs/PACKAGING.md` note
- [x] (vii) MIDI hardware input — CoreMIDI UMP protocol-1.0 port, omni-connect + hot-plug; live thru on armed instrument tracks via per-renderer SPSC rings behind an atomic fanout (offset-0 events, works while stopped, drop-newest + flush-on-drop so notes can't stick); recording shares the audio take's `PlaybackAnchor` beat math and lands MIDI clips in the same "Record Take N" undo step (punch trims audio only, v0); `midi.listInputs` + snapshot `midiInputs`/`midiEventCount` + MCP; hardware-free verification via virtual sources (`scripts/e2e-midi-record.swift`)

## M4 — Mixer & FX suite
- [x] (i) Bus routing & sends — bus tracks become real mix destinations: track output routing (master or bus), per-track sends (pre/post fader, level) into buses, bus volume/pan/mute/solo/meters in the engine graph + offline render parity; `track.setOutput` / `track.addSend|setSend|removeSend` commands + MCP + tests — **COMPLETE 2026-07-06**: the parked mid-play send-activation defect resolved (stale render-clock anchor after the rewire bounce, one-flag fix — see the RESOLVED entry under ## Blocked); live bus E2E 19/19 (a send added mid-play meters on its bus with NO transport command: within ~0.3 s for audio material, at the next note-on/loop wrap for MIDI material per the settled no-chase contract)
- [x] (ii) FX insert-chain architecture — `EffectRendering` seam + `ChainHostAU` (in-process registered AU `aufx/dwch/DAWP`, spike-proven from the SPM binary) as a permanent per-strip insert point; chain edits are atomically published snapshots, NEVER graph mutations (the M4 (i) failure class eliminated by construction — verified live: mid-play add/bypass/reorder/param with zero transport interruption); pre-fader inserts on audio/instrument/bus strips; `fx.add|remove|reorder|setBypass|setParam|describe` + 6 MCP tools; GainEffect proves the seam (bit-exact chain math); PDC-ready latency reporting (0 in v0)
- [x] (iii) Built-in FX pack 1 (dynamics & tone) — 4-band parametric EQ (RBJ biquads, TDF2 Float64, 0 dB bands bit-exact-skipped), soft-knee stereo-linked compressor (real peak detector, log-domain gain computer), 5 ms-lookahead brickwall limiter (monotonic-deque window max; `|out| ≤ ceiling` for EVERY sample by construction; first nonzero `latencySamples`, plumbed engine→store→wire per-effect); spectrum display deferred to mixer UI (vi)
- [x] (iv) Built-in FX pack 2 (space & color) — Freeverb reverb (8 damped combs + 4 allpasses/channel, pre-delay, mid/side width), stereo delay (integer lines, echo at exactly round(timeMs×rate/1000), feedback high-cut, ping-pong crossfeed), tanh saturator (−driveDb/2 dB fixed compensation, odd harmonics at H2/H3≈1e-15), stereo-linked gate (bit-exact passthrough open, true zeros closed, attack/hold/release ramps), 2-voice chorus (90° stereo / 180° inter-voice sine LFO offsets); all atomic-POD-publish RT-safe; 9 kinds on `fx.describe` + MCP; verified live (delay echoes in bounce, mid-play reverb add, −1 dB gate silence, 5-kind persistence)
- [x] (v) AU effect hosting (headless) — `HostedAUEffect` pull-render adapter behind `EffectRendering` (in-place via stash box + preallocated scratch ABL, render failure → dry passthrough); registry reuses the instrument timeout-raced prepare with strict-select on add / placeholder+warning on load; async prepare → single-strip invalidate → chain republish (never a graph rebuild); real `latencySamples` from `au.latency` (AUPeakLimiter: 96 @ 48 kHz); fullState in `.dawproj`; `fx.add kind=audioUnit` + `fx.listAudioUnits` + MCP (47 tools); found+fixed AUv2-bridge input-bus-disabled bug; plugin UI windows stay gated on M9 bundling
- [x] (vi) Full mixer view — console-style horizontal rack: channel strips (kind badge, inserts w/ bypass dots, sends w/ mini-faders, output picker, pan knob, long-throw fader w/ dB readout, mute/solo/arm glow buttons, live meter), BUSES-divided bus strips, accent-bordered pinned MASTER w/ stereo meter; `MixerModel` headless view-model in DAWAppKit (strip derivation/dB/pan/geometry, 10 tests); ARRANGE⇄MIX header toggle + `ui.showMixer` debug-tier command; Canvas controls (VerticalFader/PanKnob/SendMiniFader); design language codified as the "Mixer console" pattern in DESIGN-LANGUAGE.md; verified by captureUI self-render (agent + independent) — master insert chain deferred until DAWCore grows a master effect chain; hosted-AU insert picker UI deferred (control-plane add works)
- [x] (vii-a) Automation domain model + store CRUD — `AutomationLane/Target/Point/Curve` in DAWCore (target enum persistence-stable incl. deferred sendLevel; pure `value(atBeat:)` evaluator, canonicalized points, clamp-through-target-range), `Track.automation` additive Codable, ProjectStore CRUD (idempotent addLane w/ v0 rejections, whole-array setPoints w/ 4096 cap + `automation.points:<laneID>` coalescing, cascades drop targeting lanes inside removeEffect/removeSend/bus-delete edits), `.dawproj` persistence omitted-when-empty (pre-automation saves byte-identical); 19 tests
- [x] (vii-b) Engine read path: volume/pan lanes — `AutomationSchedule`/`AutomationRenderer` (atomic slot + ≥1s retire bin, MIDIEventSchedule pattern; preallocated cursors w/ binary-search reseek), post-chain-walk gain+pan stage in ChainHostAU + InstrumentRenderer (per-sample linear ramps — analytic bounce error 7.4e-9; pan-center bit-exact null), fader-override (mixer pinned, lane supplies gain; mute/solo gating intact) + stopped-WYSIWYG, no-restart point republish (proven: MIDI schedule object identity unchanged across mid-play edits), live/offline parity cross-diff 0.0; 9 engine tests
- [x] (vii-c) Engine read path: built-in FX-param lanes — per-quantum render-thread POD stores (quantum-start eval, `AutomationParamOverlay` base/effective split w/ knob-revert on lane removal, 64-track/strip cap matching preallocated cursors); lock-free-POD audit per kind (all nine: main-actor apply allocates → lean render-thread setter added; derive paths pure libm/arithmetic, limiter lookahead fixed-size, delay/reverb/chorus lines MAX-sized read-offset changes)
- [x] (vii-d) Control protocol + MCP — `automation.addLane|removeLane|setPoints|setLaneEnabled` (target/point wire shapes round-trip through the model's own Codable so wire never drifts from persistence; per-index point parse errors; store rejections surface verbatim), snapshot lanes ride Track's encoding for free, 12 control tests, 4 MCP tools (51 total) with AI-agent-oriented descriptions
- [x] (vii-e) Arrange automation lane UI (v0) — per-track disclosure row (cyan-glow glyph when lanes active), VOL/PAN target picker + green enable toggle + delete, Canvas breakpoint editor (neon polyline w/ glow, click-add, drag-move w/ live readout, double-click/⌫ delete, dimmed when disabled; pan lanes neutral-white per mixer convention); pure geometry/edit/selection logic headless in `DAWAppKit.AutomationLaneModel` (16 tests); all edits via vii-a store methods (per-tick drag commits ride the `automation.points:<laneID>` coalescing key); debug-tier `ui.showAutomation` for headless capture; pattern codified in DESIGN-LANGUAGE.md — **automation v0 complete** (vii-f deferred)
- [ ] (vii-f) DEFERRED post-v0: touch/latch/write recording, sendLevel engine support, AU-param lanes, master lanes, bezier curves
- [x] (viii-a) PDC plan math (DAWCore) — `LatencyCompensation.swift`: `PDCPlan.compute(input:cap:)` (`PDCStripKind.track(outputsToMaster:hasSends:)|.bus`, per-strip plannedSamples/compensationSamples/clamped/skewSamples + residual, T/B/maxPathLatency; bypass-stable maxima over all-effects sums, comp from active sums, sends pin to T, no-sends direct-to-master refinement to T+B, skew=B only for direct+sends while B>0, 16384 cap w/ honest unclamped reporting, hostile negative inputs clamped not precondition-crashed); 15 unit tests incl. spec worked example verbatim
- [x] (viii-b) Compensation ring (DAWEngine) — `CompensationDelay.swift` (`CompensationDelayState`: 32768-float pow-2 rings/channel, heap atomic target+resetFlag, render-only writeIndex/appliedOffset/historyClean; clean-history target-0 fast path provably buffer-untouched; dirty target-0 keeps writing so later retargets crossfade into real history); inserted in ChainHostAU between chain walk and automation.apply + InstrumentRenderer main AND idle paths; `PlaybackGraph.setCompensationTarget(_:forStrip:)` + `armCompensationResets()` at stopAllPlayers/startAllPlayers (covers cold start + offline start; v0 loop wrap flushes BY DESIGN — wrap is a restart where chain tails already cut; spec's no-flush rule applies when seamless wrap lands); 7 tests: impulse alignment 4800/5040→single coherent 0.5 peak, exact null, 512-bit-pattern inertness, bit-exact crossfade formula, reset kills 240-sample stale tail, determinism, instrument-path 480
- [x] (viii-c) PDC recompute wiring + reporting — single choke point at the tail of `PlaybackGraph.applyParameters` (all 6 trigger events already funnel through it; offline calls it both sides of engine start → parity by construction); `EffectChainState.latencySamplesAllEffects`; `PDCReport` (outputLatency structured for a future master chain); additive snapshot fields (per-strip chainLatencySamples/compensationSamples always, clamped/skew omit-if-false/zero; project `pdc` object); no new command (spec §6, snapshots ride existing surface; MCP passthrough untyped so no TS change); 7 wiring tests + live E2E 23/23 (bypass mid-play: totals stable, one-strip retarget, playback never stops)
- [x] (viii-d) PDC parity — latent-chain + shared-send-bus project cross-diffed across two offline renders at bit-level 0.0 with plan-correct 4-path coherent alignment (peak exactly 1.0); live-capture harness doesn't exist yet, so v0 bar = offline determinism + live E2E assertions (honest note); ARCHITECTURE settled entry landed at design time; strip latency-readout DESIGN note deferred to when the mixer grows the readout — **M4 (viii) PDC v0 COMPLETE**

## M5 — Editing depth
- [x] (i-a) Clip edit domain + store — `Clip.gainDb` (−72…+24) + `fadeInBeats`/`fadeOutBeats` + `FadeCurve.linear|equalPower` + NEW `startOffsetSeconds` (didn't exist; split/trim impossible without it), all additive omit-when-default Codable incl. ClipDocument mirror (pre-edit projects byte-identical); pure `envelopeGain(atBeat:)` (equal-power sin/cos quarter-cycle, gain×fades multiplicative — midpoints 0.5 / 0.7071 / −6dB≈0.5012 verified); store ops splitClip (fixed-tempo offset math + MIDI partition w/ overhang truncation + fade redistribution), trimClip (leading edge advances offset, drops outside notes, re-clamps fades), moveClip, setClipGain, setClipFades — clamped, undo-coalesced (`clip.trim|move|gain|fades:<id>`), proportional fade reduction when in+out > length; 17 tests / 3 suites
- [x] (i-b) Clip gain/fade engine read path — settled design implemented: `ClipFadeBake.swift` (piecePlan contiguity by construction, applyEnvelope from `Clip.envelopeGain` w/ gain zeroed, bake-owned second AVAudioFile reader — never the player's stateful streaming instance); scheduleAll three-piece buffer/segment/buffer (unfaded = pre-i-b byte-identical path; bake failure → unfaded fallback, timing over shape), startOffsetSeconds honored (bit-exact), gain = player.volume every applyParameters pass + in-place `clipGainChanged` (no restart; gainDb in NO reconcile signature; fades/offset ARE schedule-affecting → restart+re-bake); MIDI clips unreachable by construction; 12 tests: fade error 0.0, null 0/96000 frames, splice-invariance residue 2.98e-8 (1 ulp), equal-power ≤ +3.02 dB, mid-fade start exact, determinism
- [x] (i-c) Clip edit control + MCP — `clip.split|trim|move|setGain|setFades` (split returns both clips; parseFadeCurve names the offending field; store rejections verbatim), 5 MCP tools (56 total), 14 control tests, live E2E 24/24 (split note partition, snapshot round-trips, persistence, error surfaces) re-run independently ALL PASS
- [x] (i-d) Waveform editor UI — interactive ClipBlock (body drag = snapped move, ~6pt edge zones = snapped trim, double-click/context-menu split incl. at-playhead, corner fade grips w/ translucent linear/equal-power shading + alt-click curve toggle via context menu, cyan dB gain chip w/ vertical drag), SNAP header control (Off/Bar/Beat/1/2/1/4 — Bar follows the meter, hence new ClipSnap not the piano roll's fixed-bar SnapResolution), `ClipWaveform` cached off-main peak outline windowed by startOffsetSeconds; headless `ClipEditModel` in DAWAppKit (snap/hit/preview math mirroring store clamps, 14 tests); all edits via the five store methods; capture-verified (split visible, fades bowed, waveform continuous across split, −6.0 dB chips) — **M5 (i) waveform editor COMPLETE** (44 tests total across i-a…d)
- [x] (ii-a) Time-stretch library + seam design — signalsmith-stretch (MIT) DECIDED (research doc 2026-07-05; Rubber Band commercial fallback, Apple TimePitch = future RT preview only); integration seam SETTLED (ARCHITECTURE entry + scratchpad stretch-seam-spec.md): 3 additive clip fields, absolute ratio v0, full-source-file content-keyed CAF cache outside .dawproj (geometry-free keys — trim/split/move/tempo never invalidate), offset×ratio schedule mapping w/ fade bake unchanged, debounced latest-wins async render w/ silence-while-pending, identity = exact bypass
- [x] (ii-b) Vendor + facade — signalsmith-stretch v1.3.2 (57b93f4) + signalsmith-linear (7f53cdd) vendored verbatim w/ licenses + VENDORED.md pins; `CSignalsmithStretch` target (flat-C nullability-annotated API, one C++ TU, Accelerate backend, package cxx17 — no conflicts); `OfflineStretcher` facade (planar core + PCM-buffer convenience, upstream `exact()` recipe via output_seek → no post-trim, FIXED RNG seed → determinism + content-keyed-cache-ready, `isIdentity` bypass predicate excludes formant per seam rule); 8 tests: lengths EXACT (144000/72000/96000), pitch 440→440.00 / +7st→659.00 vs 659.26, formant variant, cancellation at poll 2 of ~36, bit-identical runs; FLAG for ii-d/e: 0.75× overlap-add overshoot peak 1.414 from 0.8 input (~+4.9 dB) — Float32 CAF won't clip on disk but headroom decision needed at listening spike
- [x] (ii-c) Stretch domain + surface — `Clip.stretchRatio/pitchShiftSemitones/formantPreserve` (omit-when-default + ClipDocument mirror; pure `sourceWindowSeconds(tempoBPM:)` + `isStretchIdentity` helpers), store ops `setClipStretch` (nil=keep-current, MIDI-rejected, `clip.stretch:<id>` coalesce) + `stretchClip(toLengthBeats:)` compound (window-invariant ratio scaling; ratio-clamp re-derives length so invariance survives; fades re-clamp) + split copies to both halves + trim preserves; `clip.setStretch|stretchToLength` commands + 2 MCP tools (58 total); 20 tests/+4 suites; live wire smoke PASS (clamp to 4, compound 8 beats→ratio 4, MIDI rejection verbatim, snapshot round-trip)
- [x] (ii-d) Stretch engine wire — `StretchRenderCache` (@MainActor; SHA256 content key over path/size/mtime/param-bits/engine-version, `<key>.caf` Float32 full-file renders in `~/Library/Caches/DAWPro/StretchRenders/`, 250ms debounce + per-clip latest-wins cancel + same-key single-flight, unique `.partial-<token>.caf` → atomic rename); PlaybackGraph `StretchResolution` resolver seam (ready → rendered CAF replaces source w/ `startOffsetSeconds × ratio` offset mapping, pending → silence, identity clips never touch the resolver — null test 0.0); AudioEngine owns cache + `stretchDesired` dedupe (failed renders not retried on identical params — re-edit retries), completion invalidates + restarts via `tracksDidChange`; `renderMixdown` awaits pending renders (WYSIWYG); OfflineRenderer `stretchedFileProvider` seam (nil → silent, never wrong-speed); snapshot `stretchRendering`/`stretchError` omit-when-default; 8 tests (identity null 0.0, cache hit/miss/param/mtime re-key, offset map bit-exact at frame 48000, stretched fades 0.0, latest-wins single CAF, silent-pending) + 16-check live E2E re-run independently ALL PASS (transient rendering flag, stretched window audible past source end, mid-play re-stretch resumes through restart seam) — 680/79. Deferred: cache LRU eviction sweep
- [x] (ii-e) Stretch UI + listening spike — ClipBlock ⌥-drag right-edge stretch handle (high-priority `.modifiers(.option)` gesture, live "length · ratio" readout, "≈" grip hover cue via hover-scoped NSEvent flags monitor), amber out-of-band (outside 0.75–1.5×) border/badge glow, persistent SF Mono ratio/pitch badge on non-identity clips, `ClipShimmer` animated sweep while rendering (10 Hz bounded-window AppModel poll over pull-based `clipStretchStatus`, kicked by `onChange(of: stretchSignature)` so gesture AND control edits shimmer), red border + error dot on failure; headless `ClipStretchModel` in DAWAppKit (stretchPreview mirrors store's window-invariance + clamp→length re-derive, cross-checked against the real store; 14 tests → 694/80); DESIGN-LANGUAGE patterns recorded; capture-verified (badges, amber tint, shimmer frames). Listening grid (ACE-Step absent → live-app polySynth phrase, chords+staccato): 36 cells, true peaks −7.67…−1.69 dBTP, 0/36 over 0 dBFS, lengths exact, ii-b sine overshoot did NOT reproduce on musical material (0.75× cell peaks 1.5 dB BELOW source); headroom call: no baked compensation gain — Float32 end-to-end, master-bus true-peak stage later, amber hint surfaces risk; **signalsmith-stretch stamped PROVISIONAL-FINAL for 0.75–1.5× (no Rubber Band escalation), human audition pending** (scratchpad stretch-listen/LISTENING-NOTES.md) — **M5 (ii) time-stretch COMPLETE**
- [x] (iii-a) Take/comp domain + store — `Takes.swift` (TakeLane/CompSegment/TakeGroup w/ derived rangeBeats + clamped crossfadeSeconds, pure deterministic CompFlattener), `Clip.takeGroupID` + `Track.takeGroups` (omit-when-default/empty additive Codable + ProjectDocument mirrors, lane payload = ClipDocument w/ media ref), 7 store ops in `ProjectStore+Takes.swift` (groupTakes connected-cluster overlap, setCompSegments/selectTake coalesce `take.comp:<gid>`, removeTakeLane, flattenTakeGroup→[Clip], moveTakeGroup, setTakeCrossfade) + shared `requireNotCompMember` guard in all 9 clip-edit ops (quantize ops add 1 call each when they land) + setTempo re-flatten in one performEdit + planMedia walks lane media deduped; 27 tests/+4 suites → 721/84, 0 warnings, independently verified (design: ARCHITECTURE settled entry + comping-quantize-spec.md)

- [x] Crash safety — **PARENT COMPLETE 2026-07-10** (all three sub-items landed and independently verified: teardown UAF root-caused + retire-bin fix → rolling autosave + honest crash detection + recovery offer in-app and on the wire → heartbeat watchdog driving the proven recovery path).   - [x] (crash-a) Teardown crash: root-cause + fix + regression guard — **FIXED 2026-07-10 (root cause PROVEN with a 6-experiment live evidence matrix, not conjectured)**: mechanism = AVFoundation completes a node detach's internal graph bookkeeping ONLY when it can synchronize with a running engine; detaching a once-rendered node while STOPPED leaves a stale raw `AUGraphNodeBaseV3*` in `AVAudioEngineGraph`'s internal list (survives `reset()`+`start()`; explicit disconnect-first does NOT purge it — experiments D1/D2), ARC then frees the node, and the next live `connect` (first track.add after project.new) walks freed memory. Our teardown hit it because reconcile's removal pass fires the quiesce-STOP at the first non-trivial strip, so the mass detach ran stopped-after-running. KEY INVERSION (exp C): stop-before-any-detach — the "cleanest" reading of the old discipline — still crashes; the discipline's stop IS the poison for detaches (safe direction is attach-while-stopped/cold-start; detach needs RUNNING — exp B/E clean incl. a full 28-strip live teardown). H2 refuted (every removed node had a paired detach); H3 not the trigger but the fix restores the detach-sync guarantee the renderer-deinit WATCH item leans on. FIX (minimal): `PlaybackGraph.retireNode(_:)`/`flushRetiredNodes()` + `engineHasRun` — running or never-ran → detach now (offline/test byte-identical); stopped-after-running → park attached+strongly-held in a FIFO pending-detach bin (no freed-memory window CAN exist), flushed after every successful `engine.start()` (prepare/rewire-bounce/config-recovery) + defensively at reconcile entry; every teardown detach site seam-routed incl. dead `detachAll()`; announce/bounce semantics untouched; silently covers latent same-class windows (live addSend old-gain teardown, invalidateInstrumentNode, mixed bus-removal passes). Root-cause note + evidence matrix: `docs/research/fix-teardown-crash.md` (written BEFORE the fix); repro doc status FIXED; ARCHITECTURE boundary discipline gained the lifetime rule. Regression: `TeardownRetireTests.swift` — 4 deterministic ordering pins (live crash is HAL-timing/heap-reuse dependent, unreachable headless; labeled as such). Verified: agent live 3× full-repro survived + −23.07 dB sanity; ORCHESTRATOR independent gate 5/5 — 3 consecutive teardown cycles in ONE process (16 synths + 3 buses + sends each, played) + 5 adds each + post-churn playback −24.04 dB + undo intact + ZERO new .ips; suite **1437/172** (from 1433/171) independently; isolation exactly 5 files, zero instrumentation remnants; 0 warnings. - [x] (m11-d) Arrange-level clip crossfades + overlap correctness — **COMPLETE 2026-07-11**. Fixes the audit's NEW-DISCOVERY BUG (`ProjectStore.moveClip` did no overlap detection → overlapped ordinary clips silently volume-doubled with no crossfade/error) AND ships a crossfade tool. **Policy (settled, no render change): §1** no SILENT overlap of ordinary same-track clips — only the explicit crossfade tool creates a legitimate overlap (covered by complementary fades); **§2** a move that lands on a stationary same-track clip TRIMS the covered region (full containment → the stationary clip is removed), audio+MIDI alike, comp members exempt, all inside ONE "Move Clip" undo; **§3** m10-k targeted-track import applies the same trim inside its single-undo batch (new-track placements unaffected); **§4** moving a previously-crossfaded clip re-trims against current boundaries, fades survive as plain per-clip fades. **DAWCore**: value types `ClipMoveResult {clip, trimmedClipIDs, removedClipIDs}` + `CrossfadeResult {left, right, overlapBeats}`; `moveClip` rewritten to rebuild the lane applying `resolveOverlap` to each ordinary (non-comp-member) same-track clip; statics `clipTrimmedToWindow` (mirrors `trimClip`: advances `startOffsetSeconds`, drops/truncates MIDI, clamps fades; nil below `minClipLengthBeats`) + `resolveOverlap` (disjoint→keep / full-cover→drop / head-cover→trim leading / tail-or-inside→trim trailing); `crossfadeClips(trackId, clipId, otherClipId, lengthBeats)` — AUDIO only, adjacent or overlapping ≤ length, symmetric half-each extension where source material exists (else field-named `crossfadeNeedsMaterial`), legacy-overlap normalization, complementary `equalPower` fades spanning EXACTLY the final overlap, each clip's OTHER fade preserved, ONE "Crossfade Clips" undo; `importAudioBatch` existing-track path now applies `resolveOverlap`. **Wire (+1, 114→115)**: `clip.crossfade {trackId, clipId, otherClipId, lengthBeats>0}` → `{left, right, overlapBeats}` (field-named errors `crossfadeNotEligible`/`crossfadeNeedsMaterial`); `clip.move` response gained additive `trimmed:[UUID]`/`removed:[UUID]` (existing `clip` fields byte-identical). **MCP (+1, 117→118)**: `clip_crossfade` teaching the split→butt→crossfade workflow; `clip_move` description carries the overlap policy + the additive fields. **Copilot catalog 43→44** (clip 11→12; `clip.crossfade` added, non-destructive-beyond-undo). **UI**: arrange clip context menu **"Crossfade with Next"** (¼/½/1/2-beat submenu, audio-only, only when a crossfadeable next clip exists) → `ProjectStore.crossfadeClips`; a green **X-bowtie seam badge** over each overlapping ordinary audio pair (the clips' own fade wedges shade the overlap — neutral audio green, never violet); `.crossfade` Explain entry (catalog **61→62**). **Explain overlay robustness (thin-view fix, general)**: `ExplainOverlay.cardCenter` now clamps the card center in BOTH axes so a card flipping above a high anchor (e.g. the seam badge near the ruler) can no longer clip its title off the window top. `debug.explainMode {focus:"crossfade"}` stages the capture. **GATE (staging 17695, headless WS driver)**: suite **1908/222** (+ `DAWCoreTests.ClipCrossfadeTests` 13, `DAWControlTests.ClipCrossfadeCommandTests` 7), 0 warnings incl. `--build-tests`; npm **84/84** (0 skipped, 118-tool pin exercised); live gate ALL PASS — **(a) doubling fixed, MEASURED**: single clip **−10.66 LUFS**, a second identical clip stacked on top **−4.64 LUFS** (the pre-fix bug reproduced, **+6.02 dB**), then a 50 %-overlap move trimmed the stationary clip → **−10.63 LUFS** (**afterVsSingle 0.03 dB — doubling gone**), `clip.move` returned `trimmed:[clipA]`; - [x] (m11-e) Track bounce-in-place — **COMPLETE 2026-07-11**. Render-and-land vertical over `ProjectStore.bounceTrackInPlace(trackId, fromBeat?, durationSeconds?, muteSource?, name?)` (`Sources/DAWCore/ProjectStore+Bounce.swift`), reusing `render.stems`' render machinery (full-session forced PDC, single post-fader `StemPlan.passTracks` pass, same default window, NEVER normalized — DAWEngine untouched) and `importGeneration`'s land discipline (render+write OUTSIDE the edit body into the project-stable `generationImportsDirectory`; ONE `performEdit("Bounce in Place")` inserts the `<source> (Bounced)` audio track+clip DIRECTLY AFTER the source and mutes the source when `muteSource` default-true). Eligibility is IDENTICAL to `render.stems` for one track (`StemPlan.descriptors`): bus-routed source → `stemNotMasterInput` verbatim, unknown → `trackNotFound`, empty window → `nothingToRender`; a bus bounces. Undo removes the new track+clip AND restores the source's prior mute; the rendered FILE stays on disk (import semantics). `renderCompletedCount` deliberately NOT ticked (that's the export-song onboarding signal). Result `BounceInPlaceResult {track, clip, file, sourceTrackId, sourceMuted, measurement}`. **Wire (+1, 115→116)**: `track.bounceInPlace`. **MCP (+1, 118→119)**: `track_bounce_in_place`; NOT in the Copilot catalog (long-running render op — the `render.*` exclusion precedent, documented). **UI**: track-header context menu "Bounce in Place" (master-input tracks only, both densities — no density split, no inventory row); Explain `.bounceInPlace` (catalog 62→**63**). Fix = add `gainEnvelope` to the fingerprint + `moveDelta` guard + the stale-message (`"gain envelope (N → M points)"`). Test `staleGainEnvelopeEditMidJob` (ClipFixTests). **D3 (NO CODE BUG — gate-script defect) — "non-constant envelope absent in mixdown":** the render IS correct; the repro script `verify-m13e-orch.mjs::wavSamples` read the STEREO WAV interleaved-flat without deinterleaving, so its "beat 6" index 141600 actually sampled frame 70800 = beat 2.95 (the flat 0 dB head), giving 0.0 delta; the constant control passed only because a uniform scale is index-invariant. PROVEN by (a) in-memory `channelData[0]` (already deinterleaved) RMS: A2 window −6.00 dB, A4 −10.5 dB exactly; (b) deinterleaving disk `a-ramp.wav` ch0: beat 6 = −5.9965 dB, beat 7.5 = −10.469 dB, head 0.0. Regression `nonConstantEnvelopeAppliesOnReRender` (ClipEnvelopeRenderTests) renders the SAME clip dry-THEN-enveloped (the wire's ordering, MONO 48 k PCM16 source) and asserts the ramp applies on the re-render — closing the "stale envelope-blind bake cache" hypothesis (there is no bake cache; OfflineRenderer builds a fresh graph per render). **D4 (NO CODE BUG — gate-script defect) — "bounce retains envelope → double-apply":** `bounceTrackInPlace` (ProjectStore+Bounce.swift:133) already lands a FRESH `Clip(...)` with an EMPTY envelope on a NEW "(Bounced)" track pointing to the baked stem file; the gate's B2 read `clipsOf(doc, sourceTrackId)` — the SOURCE track (correctly muted, correctly retaining its own envelope), not the bounced track. Verified live: bounced track clip `gainEnvelope=[]`, and deinterleaved b-post == b-pre at every beat (no double-apply). Staging re-swept per law (.session.lock cleared, .ips 20→20). - [x] (m13-h2) **Envelope-bake perf follow-up** (filed from the m13-e audio-dsp review — correctness is NOT at stake, the null/analytic gates all pass): a non-empty gain envelope currently converts the clip's bake plan to ONE full-region baked piece, so `bakePiece` (PlaybackGraph.swift ~:1710) allocates and per-frame-evaluates the entire scheduled region on the main actor at EVERY `scheduleAll` (play/seek/loop restart) — ~230 MB + ~29 M `envelopeGain` calls (per-frame `pow` + O(points) scan) for a 10-min stereo 48 k clip. Candidate fixes (pick via measurement, audio-dsp-engineer): piecewise bake only the inter-point spans whose gain ≠ unity (mirror the fade three-piece plan), hoist the dB→linear `pow` to per-ramp incremental multiplication, and/or cache the baked buffer keyed by (file, shape, envelope) across scheduleAll calls. GATE: perf measurement before/after on a long enveloped clip (bake time + peak RSS at scheduleAll), null-case byte gate era, analytic envelope render tests unchanged. — **COMPLETE 2026-07-12 (audio-dsp-engineer).** Fix chosen BY MEASUREMENT: **piecewise bake** (`ClipFadeBake.envelopedPiecePlan` + `PlaybackGraph.scheduleEnvelopedPieces`) — only spans the envelope/fades actually shape are baked (±1 guard frame, streamed gaps < 8_192 frames fold into the bake); provably-unity spans stream straight off the file, bit-identical to the old `× 1.0` multiply, so rendered bytes are UNCHANGED in every case (not just null). MEASURED (release, 10-min stereo 48 k clip, 4-beat dip, `OfflineRenderer` 0.25 s pull ≡ one scheduleAll): mostly-unity **191.5 ms → 40.6 ms** median (dry floor 38.8 ms; bake cost ~153 ms → ~1.5 ms), peak RSS **287 MB → 20 MB** (dry 18 MB); flat-0 dB envelope 203 → 39.2 ms (zero bake); full-non-unity stays ~205 ms/284 MB (envelope genuinely shapes everything — honest cost; pow-hoist + cache REJECTED: read+alloc dominates, numerics/invalidation risk buys nothing in the common case). Byte gates all four SHA-identical before/after (null `0adcccbd…`, enveloped `83f2e4c1…`, mid-seek `3d939bf3…`, Bus Song bundle COPY `1d9e5e3f…`); m13-e analytic/null tests pass UNMODIFIED (unity-envelope residue now exactly 0.0). Order: a → b → c (correctness; independent of each other) → d → e (features) → f (spike) → g → h → i (debt/docs). Audit takeaway worth pinning: "the biggest wins were things the wire already did that no human could reach, and the worst bugs were on the newest and the oldest seams, not the middle."

## M14 — Gapless loop wrap (seeded 2026-07-12 from the m13-f design spike: docs/research/design-m13f-gapless-loop.md, GO-WITH-CONDITIONS; implementation follows that doc's §9 phases L-1…L-4 and §10 conditions C1–C8 verbatim — deviations return to the design doc for amendment)

**Standing law (C1)**: `GaplessLoopSpikeTests` (the L-0 splice-primitive pins, 4 tests) stays green forever; any splice regression blocks M14 work that day and converts the milestone to NO-GO/park with the spike retained as evidence (m10-p precedent). **Standing law (C4)**: zero new RT surface beyond the bounded cursor re-seek — no allocation, locks, or ObjC on the render path in ANY phase; any deviation returns to the design doc for amendment. Offline/render parity (§7): nothing changes offline, ever — provably (C8).

- [x] (m14-a / L-1) **Transport core** — AudioEngine + PlaybackGraph, control thread only: loop window in `scheduleAll`, per-cycle unrolled audio segments + baked-buffer cache, `derivedBeats` modular branch + timeline law, playhead-task top-up (`scheduledThroughCycle`), the wrap path stops calling `restart` (the graph never stops at wrap). Route: audio-dsp-engineer (design §2, §4 Option A, §8 failure modes 2–4). GATES: C1 spike suite green; C3 cycle-placement exactness — ≥3 unrolled cycles under a MULTI-SEGMENT tempo map, every audio anchor frame == the absolute integral with == pins (m12-c discipline; any `previous + loopFrames` accumulation found in review is a defect); C6 horizon law — schedule-ahead ≥ 2 playhead-tick periods, a 0.25-beat loop at 400 BPM sustains N ≥ 20 cycles with no starvation gap; C8 offline null-case — a non-looping project renders byte-identical (SHA) before/after, stems/bounce gates (Σ ≤ 1e-4, byte-identity) unaffected; C4. — **COMPLETE 2026-07-12, ALL GATES PASS + ONE MEASURED DESIGN AMENDMENT** (audio-dsp-engineer; orchestrator re-ran the suite, re-derived the C3 integral arithmetic by hand — cycle 108 000 frames, all 8 anchors exact — and mtime-proved wire untouched). Production surface = exactly 2 files (PlaybackGraph.swift, AudioEngine.swift) + GaplessLoopTransportTests(6). Mechanism per design names: `LoopWindow` in scheduleAll (:1632/:1697, nil = byte-identical linear path), `buildLoopUnroll`/`buildCyclePlan`/`enqueueLoopCycle` (anchors = absolute integral, never previous+loopFrames), baked fade/envelope pieces cached ONCE and re-enqueued per cycle, `beat(forElapsedSeconds:)` modular branch + `LoopContext` integrals, `serviceLoop` 33 ms top-up → `topUpLoopCycles` with `scheduledThroughCycle`; restart survives ONLY for loop edits/enable-mid-play (one seam, then gapless). **THE AMENDMENT (design §4-A + §8 modes 8–9, doc updated)**: "wrap-minus-margin" pre-queue is measured-UNSAFE — (8) drained-queue freeze: a strip-chain player whose queue fully drains never sounds later-queued items at ANY lead (33 696 frames still silent; bare player→mainMixer does NOT reproduce it, which is how L-0 missed it); (9) mid-flight splice needs ≥ ~2.5k frames of lead (item lost ≤2048, partial ~2300, clean ≥2496; L-0's 2928 margin sat just above the cliff). Remedy inside Option A: eager top-up ≥ max(horizon, sounding+2). - [x] (m16-b1) **MIDI CC + pitch bend — the design doc (audit F9/§4, the two-audit-running model gap).** ✅ **COMPLETE 2026-07-13** — docs/research/design-m16b-midi-cc.md (324 lines, GO-WITH-CONDITIONS, C1–C20; grounds are structural: stuck sustain is unusable output, not teachable; without chase, playback state depends on the PREVIOUS roll (HostedAUInstrument.reset() sends only CC123/120 — bend/CC persist) which breaks offline==live by construction; one build-time main-actor mechanism answers seek-chase, loop wrap (each cycle block chases at loop.startBeat for free), m14-d prune self-containment, and the split seam; the note NO-CHASE guard survives verbatim (intervals vs step functions — different data, different contracts). **MODEL**: `Clip.controllerLanes: [MIDIControllerLane]` non-optional-[]-default encoded-when-non-empty (gainEnvelope mechanism); lane = {type: .cc(controller:)/.pitchBend/.channelPressure (AutomationTarget discriminator precedent), points: identity-free {beat, value}} — the F8d id-copy trap dissolved by construction; raw MIDI domains, stepwise semantics, single-channel v1; schedule kinds 2/3/4, ONE data rule (pitch≡data1, velocity≡data2). **MEASURED DECIMATION BOUND** (staging probe): per-event drain ≈1.1–1.8 µs; 8192 events/quantum OVERRUNS (11.74 ms vs 10.67 budget — and that burst is wire-reachable TODAY with 4096 same-beat notes, a pre-existing pathology; reframed the policy from prevent to bound-at-same-envelope); ~1024/quantum ≈17% safe; policy: capture thins ≥5 ms/lane + duplicate-drop (final value kept), wire caps 16 lanes/clip + 16384 points/lane, build coalesces same-frame per lane. **DISCOVERED TRAPS** (b2 must fix): the `count / 2` noteID base silently double-books noteIDs across cycle blocks once non-pair events exist (fix specced, C5-pinned); Delivery = an app-wide `NSEvent` LOCAL key-down monitor in AppModel (the TimelineLanesView ⌥-tracking precedent) — deliberately NOT a menu key equivalent or `.keyboardShortcut(.space)`, because key equivalents are checked BEFORE text insertion and would steal the space bar from every rename field (the exact failure the focus guard prevents); focus guard classifies the TARGET window's `firstResponder` (`NSText` = the shared field editor behind every TextField, + an `NSTextInputClient` catch-all; MEASURED live: rest = the NSWindow itself → none, focused rename = `_SystemTextFieldFieldEditor` → text-editing); main-window-only via a weak `contentWindow` latched in `applyWindowFloor()` (first appearance = the only window, can never latch a plugin panel). **R-for-record NOT taken — not free**: the record button carries a disabled-when-unarmed guard + surfaced refusal reasons, and "R" is the established track-header ARM labeling (`recordHelp`: "arm a track (R) first") — a bare R record toggle would collide with both. `debug.keySpace` staging seam (app tier, off `allCommands`/MCP — **ZERO wire growth**, space is a UI driver for the existing `transport.play`/`stop` funnels): `{}` pure state read (monitor/window/responder-class/fieldText/transport), `{press:true}` synthesizes the NSEvent and runs the SAME `handleKeyDownEvent` body the live monitor runs (modifier/repeat/`noWindow` matrix overrides), `{press:true, post:true}` posts through the REAL event queue (live monitor fires; a passed-through space genuinely reaches the responder chain). GATES: live battery **38/38** on 17695 (stopped→play FROM beat 8 no-rewind + playhead advancing wire-proven + snapshot agreement; playing→stop parks; ⌘/⌥/⌃/⇧/repeat/no-window pass-throughs; record→space stops the take; **G3 fully live, no unit-pin fallback**: `debug.markerRename` focuses a real rename field → seam reads `text-editing` + fieldText, direct press = passThrough + transport untouched, POSTED spaces genuinely type into the field — first replaces the select-all selection (measured real-typing semantics), second APPENDS — transport never moves; posted space with no field focused toggles through the live monitor; m17-c pointer legs re-run green: zone/ghost/click-seek/split [8+4][12+4] ONE undo); suites **2508/288** (+11/+1) at 0 warnings forced-recompile; pins 126/129/56 re-grepped, `keySpace` = ZERO occurrences in Commands.swift; .ips 20→20. - [ ] (m17-i) **MLX-native ACE-Step spike (research first; user asked 2026-07-16 whether the model can be embedded natively via Apple Neural Engine/MLX instead of the external sidecar).** Position recorded: ANE (Core ML) is NOT viable for this model class (multi-billion-param diffusion transformer; ANE wants small static-shape fp16 nets) — the plausible native path is MLX on the GPU. IN-PROCESS embedding stays REJECTED regardless of framework: the main process owns the RT audio engine, a model spiking tens of GB of unified memory + GPU contention in-process risks dropouts, and a model crash must never be a DAW crash (M16 lesson) — heavy AI belongs out-of-process. The REAL candidate: replace the Python/FastAPI sidecar with a NATIVE MLX helper process (mlx-swift, or minimal Python-MLX as a stepping stone) IF a quality MLX port of ACE-Step-1.5 exists. Research **DELIVERED 2026-07-16** (docs/research/2026-07-16-ace-mlx-native.md; orchestrator spot-checked the ACEStepClient:16-26 citation — exact, the sidecar speaks ACE-Step's upstream job-queue API): **VERDICT NO-GO on a Swift/mlx-swift helper now — WAIT.** No diffusion-music model class exists in Swift MLX anywhere (mlx-swift-examples = LLM/VLM/embeddings/SD-image only; mlx-audio-swift = TTS/STT/STS/codecs); every existing ACE-Step MLX path (official 1.5 hybrid, `mlx-community/ACE-Step1.5-MLX` weights via mlx-audio, community forks) terminates in Python; cold-start is weight-load-dominated (8–20+ GB from disk — a Swift rewrite pays the same), and the ANE ceiling is confirmed ~1–1.3B params (Core ML SD precedent) vs ACE-Step's 5–9B+ pipeline. RE-CHECK trigger: mlx-audio-swift or mlx-swift-examples shipping ANY diffusion-audio model class. NEAR-TERM alternative flagged and folded into m17-h's decision space (not a separate build): the coarse progress is a limitation of the upstream FastAPI job-queue API — a days-scale Python-only spike driving `mlx_audio`'s loader directly could yield true per-step progress and skip the HTTP queue. This item stays UNCHECKED as the WAIT tripwire; no implementation scheduled.

## M18 — Hardening & polish (seeded 2026-07-16 by the orchestrator from the filed follow-up pool after M17 closed; every item cites its filing) — **MILESTONE COMPLETE 2026-07-16 (a–i all verified)**

- [x] (m18-a) **RSS churn leak under rebuild storms (filed: m16-h C3 soak).** Measured ground truth: ~9.7 MB/iteration LINEAR RSS growth under adversarial `project.new`/rebuild churn — 114 MB → 985 MB over 90 storm iterations. Long AI-agent sessions do exactly this kind of churn, so the leak compounds in real use. The suite was ALWAYS latently device-rate-dependent; prior runs just sat on 48 kHz devices. My initial "Apple AU environment shift" attribution was WRONG — corrected here. Offline render paths pin 48 kHz and are unaffected (m19-b wire-gate mixdowns reported 48000 with AirPods connected). - [x] (m19-k) **Architecture review: should the live graph follow the device rate at all? (filed from m19-j Task 3).** Today the entire live graph's processing rate follows `outputNode.outputFormat(forBus:0)` — whatever the default device is. A Bluetooth headset entering mic mode drags the whole graph to 24 kHz: every insert chain re-prepares (limiter lookahead halves, PDC recomputes), hosted AUs hit the R7 synchronous renegotiation (bounded main-actor stalls, now bank-gated), and monitoring is band-limited to 12 kHz while the project and every offline render stay 48 kHz. Question: project-rate live graph with explicit mainMixer→outputNode resampling (the pro-DAW norm) — making chain latencies, PDC, and automation math device-invariant by construction (the whole m19-j sensitivity class disappears), with exact live/offline parity and no AU re-prepare storms on device swaps. Known costs (from the m19-j diagnosis): one SRC stage on the live path; a policy question for genuinely high-rate interfaces (96 k); capture edge still needs the device rate; several `graphFormat()` call sites assume graph rate == output-node rate and need a one-by-one audit. Include in scope: the m19-j residual (`Loudness.measure` synchronous on the main actor post-render — hop to a detached task; RenderedAudio is a value type). Route: daw-architect (design first, no code). GATE: a design doc in docs/research/ with a GO/NO-GO and migration plan. — **DONE 2026-07-16, daw-architect single flight, DESIGN-ONLY** (doc is the flight's only write — freeze verified). Doc: `docs/research/2026-07-16-m19k-device-rate-design.md` (572 lines). **Verdict 1 (big question): GO, probe-gated** — both load-bearing SDK behaviors are header-DOCUMENTED, not folklore: AVAudioIONode.h ~:271 "you may set [the input scope] to a different format, in which case the node will convert" and AVAudioEngine.h ~:885-891 "The nodes remain attached and connected with previously set formats … in an output only chain, the output node supports rate conversion" — BOTH quotes verbatim-verified by the orchestrator against the installed SDK. Given the repo's three adverse priors on undocumented AVAudioEngine semantics (m18-d/m16-a/m19-f), the rate flip ships only behind a Phase-0 live probe (5 legs, pass thresholds fixed in-doc so they can't be goal-post-moved, designed fallback shape = documented mixer-input SRC, abort ladder → hybrid alternative with evidence attached). **Verdict 2 (Loudness.measure rider): GO, unconditional** — pure static function over `Sendable` RenderedAudio, all six call sites in `async throws` enclosures (every anchor orch-verified: Render :40/:84/:106/:194/:221, Bounce :117), explicit `Task.detached` hop chosen for SE-0338/SE-0461 executor-semantics immunity, per-site ordering analysis shows zero new hazard classes. - [x] (m21-e) **Imported-audio analysis for AI composition (design first).** Today an agent loading a full music file can get transients (`clip.detectTransients`, spectral-flux), loudness (`render.measureLoudness`), master RMS/peak (`mixer.masterAnalysis`), stems (`extract_stems`) and groove (`groove.extract`) — but NO key, chord, tempo, or spectral-balance read, so "add matching tracks to this song" has no harmonic/tempo ground truth (MIDI is fully readable; audio is not). Honest scope note: multi-segment tempo maps retune at the next control-plane intent after a mid-roll boundary crossing, never on the render thread (documented at adoptDelayTempo + OfflineRenderer).*
- [ ] (m22-g) **Reference-track workflow (EchoJay's "Reference Tracks"/"AI Compare"/"A/B", ours to design natively).** Import a reference audio file into a dedicated project slot (never a mixing track; excluded from bounce), offline-analyze it once (integrated LUFS/true peak/LRA + average 24-band spectrum + stereo width when m22-d lands), store results in the project; A/B monitor toggle (reference bypasses the master chain, level-matched to the mix's integrated LUFS); comparison surface (mix vs ref spectrum overlay + delta readouts) + copilot catalog teaching so "compare my mix to the reference" is a first-class AI move. ## Blocked

- **m20-b output-edge SRC probe — waiting on a USER decision: no loopback audio device installed.** Checked 2026-07-16 via system_profiler: present are AirPods Pro, MacBook Pro mic/speakers, phone/display mics, and ZoomAudioDevice — no BlackHole/Soundflower-class loopback. ZoomAudioDevice is deliberately NOT used (it belongs to the user's Zoom install; the probe must set the test device's nominal rate, and doing that to a real app's virtual device risks their calls — the never-touch-real-devices rule applies). To unblock: user approves installing BlackHole 2ch (e.g. `brew install blackhole-2ch`) or installs any loopback device themselves; the probe then proceeds per the m19-k design §6. Downstream: m20-d (Phase 2 rate flip) stays HARD-GATED on this probe; m20-c (Phase 1 injection) is NOT blocked and proceeds.

- **M10 (m10-p-1…6) voice conversion — HuggingFace large-binary fetch blocked by corp TLS-interception proxy** — noted 2026-07-11 at the m10-p-1 spike: every neural asset RVC needs (ContentVec/HuBERT encoder 360.8 MB, RMVPE pitch extractor 172.8 MB, generic non-personal Applio base pretrains 69.7/136.3 MB) lives on HF's LFS/CDN path, which hard-times-out under the proxy on every route tried (direct `huggingface.co/resolve/…`, `hf-mirror.com`, HTTP/1.1 forced). Plain PyPI and HF's small API/raw endpoints work fine — this is specifically a large-binary/LFS block, and it gates inference AND training identically on either engine (same files). Everything software-side is already proven (venv recipe, MLX GPU + MPS backends live — see docs/research/spike-m10p-vc.md incl. exact URLs/byte sizes in "Exact install shape for p-2"). PRECEDENT: the 55 GB ACE-Step weights DID download onto this machine previously — the block is likely a network-window condition (e.g. corp VPN on/off), not permanent. To unblock: on an unproxied network, fetch the four files from `huggingface.co/IAHispano/Applio` per the spike doc and re-run the spike's measurement half (fast — install is reproducible), then p-2…p-6 proceed. Also resolve before shipping: the MLX fork's missing LICENSE file (pyproject claims MIT; `gh repo view` licenseInfo null). **UNBLOCK CONFIRMED 2026-07-17 (orchestrator re-probe during the post-M20 survey)**: the network-window prediction above was correct — byte-range pulls against BOTH previously-blocked shapes now succeed with HTTP 206 (`lengyue233/content-vec-best/resolve/main/pytorch_model.bin` 10 MB at 2.4 MB/s sustained; the exact `IAHispano/Applio/resolve/main/Resources/predictors/rmvpe.pt` URL from blocker-evidence #1, 2 MB at ~1 MB/s). All ~800 MB of required assets ≈ under 15 min at these rates. m10-p-1 spike measurement half re-launched same day.
- ~~M4 (i) live mid-play send activation~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-06** (diagnostic round 3, per the parked method: stderr instrumentation + node-connection dump + preallocated-atomic tap probes + the live `diag-send.mjs` repro). Root cause was NOT the send wiring: the connection dump immediately after the rewire resume showed the mid-play-added leg fully attached and connected (source mixer → gain(vol 0.5) → bus sum → chain host → bus mixer, 48 kHz/2ch throughout) and the gain node's tap FIRING — carrying peak 0.0. Two stacked mechanisms produced the "silent until stop/play" symptom, on ALL strips (bus A metered 0.0000 after the resume too — the old E2E's poll windows just never caught it): (1) **THE BUG** — the resume anchored `derivedBeats` on `outputNode.lastRenderTime`, which right after the stop→reset→start bounce still reports the PREVIOUS render session's sample clock (valid flags set, measured sample=98304) while the restarted session's clock begins again near 0; the `max()` clamp then froze the playhead at the resume beat for the ENTIRE prior session length (unbounded in a long session — why it read as "silent forever"), postponing the loop-wrap revival past every poll (predicted wrap +4.19 s vs observed +4.17 s, 36 ms match). (2) The repro material (7.5-beat sustained MIDI chord) has no note-on between the resume beat and the wrap, and no-chase is the settled v0 contract (`MIDIEventSchedule`, ARCHITECTURE.md), so the resumed schedule was legitimately silent until the wrap — "stop/play revives it" was simply a restart from beat 0 with fresh note-ons, not a topology repair. FIX (one flag): the rewire resume calls `startPlayers(…, renderClockTrusted: false)`, forcing the already-proven host-clock anchor branch (host time is monotonic across the bounce; players start on hostTime anchors in both branches, so nothing else changes). Live post-fix: MIDI pad send meters on B at +2.29 s (= the wrap, level exactly matching the stop/play reference, no transport command, A uninterrupted-then-revived per the restart contract); audio-clip send meters at +0.26 s with A continuously intact; bus E2E 19/19 (fx-poll window widened to cover the no-chase wrap, with comment); suite 920/117 green; app stderr clean.
- ~~Teardown crash: `project.new` after a played send/bus project~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-12 (m13-a) — the crash class is dead BY CONSTRUCTION: once-rendered engines are never surgically detached; teardown-class changes discard and rebuild the whole engine.** Full arc, kept as the institutional record: **(1) 2026-07-06, discovery** during M4 (i) verification — build track→busA output + send→busB, `transport.play` ~1 s, `stop`, `project.new`, next `track.add` → SIGSEGV inside `-[AVAudioEngine connect:to:format:]` → `AVAudioEngineGraph::UpdateGraphAfterReconfig` → `swift_unknownObjectRelease` on a garbage pointer (`DAWApp-2026-07-06-051956.ips`; a sibling run crashed in a SwiftUI executor check, `…-051559.ips` — two surface stacks = heap corruption); the never-played variant did not crash. **(2) 2026-07-10, M9 crash-a fix** — diagnosis "detach against a stopped engine is unsafe"; mechanism = retire bin (`pendingDetachNodes` parked while stopped, `flushRetiredNodes()` after restart); live-verified 3× that day. **(3) 2026-07-12, FALSIFICATION** — the M13 audit (audit-m13.md B1) hit 3/3 staging sessions SIGSEGV'ing inside the fix's OWN flush path, and the m13-a C0 instrumented experiment named the mechanism with node-level evidence: after ONE engine stop→reset→start boundary, the FIRST flush-detach — of the routed source's strip mixer, with the engine RUNNING and `isRunning=true` logged at the call — is itself the faulting frame (instrumented addr `0x9ba885060 AVAudioMixerNode`, no survive line, `DAWApp-2026-07-12-104059.ips`; independently reproduced via `track.remove`, `…-104254.ips`). So "running at detach time" was NEVER sufficient: a node that RENDERED and then sat attached across a stop→reset→start boundary is already stale inside `AVAudioEngineGraph`'s internal node vector, and any later detach of it faults. The audit's "m12-f regression" suspicion was WRONG — same crash on the pre-m12-f binary; M9's 3× verification was heap-reuse luck. The C0 control leg (fresh-launch `project.new` ×20, engine never ran) survived 20/20, formally retiring the audit's session-3 "crash on first wire command" anomaly as mis-attribution (that shape cannot reach the crashing frame; plausible source = a foreign wire client, the documented 2026-07-11 staging-port anomaly). **(4) Resolution (m13-a; design docs/research/design-m13a-teardown-crash.md, supersedes fix-teardown-crash.md)** — retire-bin machinery deleted; announce-class reconcile on a once-rendered engine ABORTS before the first topology mutation and `AudioEngine.rebuildEngine(reason:)` discards the whole AVAudioEngine + PlaybackGraph and cold-builds from the model; `projectWillReplace()` forces the same rebuild unconditionally at project boundaries; `teardownDetach` detaches directly only against a running or never-run engine. Proven by the m13-a campaign: audit recipes verbatim + 12/12 played/unplayed × routed/plain matrix + 3× 41-track perf-c + 50-cycle soak (100 rebuilds, +0.4 MB RSS) + 20× fresh-launch — zero crashes, zero new .ips, m12-b offline anchors byte-identical, worst 41-track rebuild 143 ms.
- ~~AUv3 plugin view hosting (M3 vi-b)~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-10.** Unparked once pkg-a shipped the real bundle; landed as vi-b-1 (plumbing + generic body) and vi-b-2 (vendor-view ladder) — see the M3 checkboxes and `docs/research/design-vi-b-au-windows.md`. Residual, recorded honestly: no AUv3 exists on this machine, so the out-of-process AUv3 custom-view leg is untested by necessity (SKIPPED, never faked); the ladder degrades to the generic body + warning by design if one ever fails to serve a view.
- ~~Input device selection: pinned-device capture yields empty takes~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-05.** Root cause was NOT the eager pin wedging the AUHAL (disproved by CLI repro: eager prepare + pin still delivers tap buffers). Two stacked bugs: (1) the same-device guard compared the pin target against the AUHAL's `CurrentDevice`, which on a fresh AVAudioEngine is the engine's PRIVATE AGGREGATE device — never equal to any raw hardware ID — so every pinned take (default uid included) performed a real device set; (2) that set makes AVFoundation post `AVAudioEngineConfigurationChange` on the capture engine ~65 ms after start with the engine still running and the tap still healthy, and the config-change handler treated it as fatal → `stopRecording()` finalized the writer before the first buffer, and the writer's post-finalize guard silently swallowed every later delivery (hence zero frames AND zero stderr). Fix: pin skips when the uid resolves to the current system default (`InputDevices.defaultInputDeviceID()`); config-change handler only ends the take when the capture engine actually stopped; two-phase `InputCapture.prepare()/start(writer:)` replaces the eager pin; 1.5 s first-buffer watchdog aborts loudly ("no audio arrived from input device …") instead of a silent empty take. Live E2E green: default-uid pin, ZoomAudioDevice pin (frames flowed), unpinned.
- ~~Lyrics workshop real-key gate~~ **RESOLVED 2026-07-11**: the (m10-a) parser fix landed and the orchestrator ran the exact unblock condition — one real `ai.writeLyrics` (staging 17695, Keychain Anthropic key, 5.3 s, provider=anthropic) returned well-formed bracketed [verse]/[chorus] lyrics, eyeballed, 7/7 checks → M6 Lyrics workshop box CHECKED. rail-e and ex-c are now the next runnable gates; glass-b still waits on an OpenAI key. Original entry — noted 2026-07-10: no Anthropic/OpenAI API key is present on this machine (neither env nor Keychain), so the workshop lands STUB-VERIFIED only (request shapes pinned against stub servers; full vertical tested with fakes) and its box stays unchecked until a real key exists. To unblock: paste a key in Settings (⌘, — Keychain-backed, added 2026-07-10) or set `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`/`OPENAI_API_KEY`, then run one real `ai.writeLyrics` and check the output is well-formed bracketed lyrics. Same blocker applies to the copilot rail's provider calls later in M6. **UPDATE 2026-07-11: an Anthropic key is NOW present in the Keychain** (confirmed by the beta user's real provider call, which surfaced the (m10-a) parser bug) — this gate, rail-e, and ex-c become runnable as soon as (m10-a) lands. glass-b still waits on an OpenAI key.
